        )  . _:   17 years later ...  Skin is back and give you a new      :
              )_  ascii-art demonstration called :  " Fields of War "      :
             ( (                                                           :
          ( . )         __                                                 :
         )     \_      / \_    In the year 2O1O i found in www a awesome   :
           )  ___\__  <   /    Site for the real ascii  buisness  called   :
          ( ) \        \_/     Ascii  Arena  ( www . asciiarena . com ).   :
          / )  \                                                           :
         / \  /                                                       ____/
        / : \ \      This  Collection is a Tribute to the Ascii     __\
        \ o / _\     Arena .  A excelent website with a archive     \  _____
       _ \|/  \      of   thousands  ascii   collections    and      \_\   :
       |\_|  _|      inspired me to paint new ascii´s.                     :
       | :.\/|                                                            _:
       | : . |                                                            \_
      (  ..  |         In the last years i design Websites and Logos.      :
       )  :  |         But my love  to the Ascii-Art has never ended.      :
      (_ : . :                                                             :
       |)    |                                                             :
      (   )_(\_  Many  Peoples  are now  thinking " Hey grandpa why this   :
     __|___)__/_ collection? ".   And   i   say  :   " I   dont   know .   :
     \\ /__ \_ / But i love making nostalgic things like dwarf throwing :) :
      \_______/                                                            :
       |/  -\|                                                             :
       |\___/|             Indeed ASCII iS NOT DEAD and it gives so much   :
    .  |/o  \|     _____   more ideas to paint.                            :
    o  |\___/| .   \  __\                                     ------       :
